/*
  Because this file is not proccessed by our brandable_css sass pipeline,
  it cannot use our sass-direction helpers. So we have to handle RTL manually
  by putting direction-specific styles in [dir="ltr"] or [dir="rtl"] blocks.
*/

/* good menu widths */
.mejs-sourcechooser-selector {
  width: 160px;
}

  width: 160px !important;
}

  width: 105px;
}

[dir="rtl"]  .mejs-captions-selector { text-align: right }

  width: 70px !important;
}

  float: left;
}

  margin-left: 0px;
  margin-right: 5px;
  float: right;
}

    <h2>Instructions</h2>
    <div class="description user_content enhanced" role="region" aria-label="Quiz Instructions">
      <div style="width: 98%; max-width: 1000px;">
<p><img style="float: right; padding-left: 10px;" src="https://canvas.oregonstate.edu/courses/1999701/files/110922649/download" alt="" width="78" height="75" data-decorative="true" loading="lazy" data-id="110922649"></p>
<h2 style="border-bottom: 2px solid #dc4405; font-size: 18pt; margin-right: 85px;">Instructions</h2>
<p>This graded quiz, consisting of multiple-choice, true-false, and fill-in-the-blank questions, will cover various topics explored in Week 4. During Week 4, we examined the services provided by the Transport Layer and delved into some of its implementation details.</p>
<p>You are allowed <strong>two</strong> attempts at this quiz.</p>
